We do however use many of these to override the bootstrap variables below.

Original variables can be found at bootstrap/variables

Below is only the variables we have chosen to override for GoComics.
A full list of all available variables to override are located in:
/gems/bootstrap-4.1.1/assets/stylesheets/bootstrap/_variables.scss.

NOTE 1: When updating variables, remove the !default flag so that our override functions as expected. Commented out variables with the !default flag are original versions left in for visibility and ease of editing.

NOTE 2: The first variable instantiated is the value that gets applied to the rendered CSS.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------*/
